There\u2019s a new (very simple) demo at <https:\/\/github.com\/fulcrologic\/websockets2-demo>. I\u2019ll probably be porting the formal websockets-demo to this soon, but the new support is *much* cleaner, and will be much simpler to tune up to be a really nice API. \n\nAt the moment, it should be considered alpha quality, and it is currently only available in 2.2.0-SNAPSHOT on clojars.\n\nThe nicest parts: It\u2019s sooo much easier to use. Easy server setup is just:\n\n```\n(defn build-easy-server [path]\n  (easy\/make-fulcro-server\n    :config-path path\n    :components {:websockets       (fulcro.websockets\/make-websockets (fulcro.server\/fulcro-parser))\n                 :ws-adapter          (fulcro.websockets\/make-easy-server-adapter)}))\n```\n\nand the client no longer needs any wiggy stuff\u2026you pass the network state \u201cwatcher\u201d and push handler as functions, so it is much easier too:\n\n```\n(new-fulcro-client\n                ; replace the default remote with websockets\n                :networking {:remote (fw\/make-websocket-networking \"\/chsk\"\n                                       :push-handler push-handler\n                                       :state-callback state-callback)})\n```\n\nOld version needed core async, did all sorts of weird multimethod backflips, was hard to integrate with any kind of server, and didn\u2019t deal with network errors correctly. It was also quite a bit more code. \n\nIntegrating into your own web stack is also a breeze. Just inject the websockets component into your component that builds your ring stack, and then:\n\n```\n(defrecord Middleware [ring-stack websockets]\n  component\/Lifecycle\n  (start [this]\n    (assoc this :ring-stack\n                (-&gt; (not-found-handler)\n                  (fulcro.websockets\/wrap-api websockets)\n                  (wrap-keyword-params) ;required\n                  (wrap-params) ; required\n                 ...\n                  (wrap-not-modified)\n                  (wrap-gzip))))\n  (stop [this]))```\n\nI\u2019ve also done a first pass at rewriting the internal logging of Fulcro. I don\u2019t recommend it for general use, but I\u2019m trying to get rid of the timbre dependency. The new logging using println (clj) and glog (cljs)\u2026so there\u2019s no real external library overhead. Having a little trouble getting line nubmers to work right\u2026works fine in the tests, but not in the wild. Anyway, it should not break things (the old namespace is still there), but during transition other libraries might continue to use the old namespace, which dynamically loads timbre\u2026so you may still need it as a dep for the time being (e.g. fulcro-datomic still uses it at the moment). I\u2019ll be fixing up other libraries to use the new support as soon as possible.","ts":"1518147775.000102","user":"U0CKQ19AQ","type":"message"},"type":"message","hidden":true,"channel":"C68M60S4F","previous_message":{"edited":{"user":"U0CKQ19AQ","ts":"1518148203.000000"},"attachments":[{"thumb_width":211,"thumb_height":211,"service_name":"GitHub","title_link":"https:\/\/github.com\/fulcrologic\/websockets2-demo","fallback":"GitHub: fulcrologic\/websockets2-demo","from_url":"https:\/\/github.com\/fulcrologic\/websockets2-demo","title":"fulcrologic\/websockets2-demo","id":1,"thumb_url":"https:\/\/avatars3.githubusercontent.com\/u\/30102823?s=400&v=4","service_icon":"https:\/\/a.slack-edge.com\/bfaba\/img\/unfurl_icons\/github.png","text":"websockets2-demo - Demo of websocket support as of version 2.2+ of Fulcro"}],"text":"[message text edited or deleted]","ts":"1518147775.000102","user":"U0CKQ19AQ","type":"message"}}
